The scenery is unparalleled, with beautiful lakes and mountains. The national canoeing team training base is here, and the scenes of athletes training add to the dynamic picture of the scenery. The hotel is the first 5-star hotel in Changde. It is high-end and luxurious. The rooms are large and the facilities, equipment and sanitary services are very good. The western restaurant of Zhiwei Restaurant on the 14th floor has a great view. The Chinese food is distinctive, especially the wild lake fish of Liuye Lake is very delicious. , staying in the hotel will give you a free cruise ticket for 2 people. It is very convenient to walk to the cruise terminal in 3 minutes. It was a good experience and worth staying again.
